<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плюнуть.html>плю́нуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pljúnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плевать.html>плева́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to spit
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:плюнуть.html>плю́нуть</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">raz <b>pljúnutʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">piece of cake</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to spit upon, to not care for</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:плюс.html>плюс</a> (15718)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">plūs</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">more</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плюс.html>плюс</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pljus</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плюс.html>плю́са</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плюс.html>плю́сы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плюс.html>плю́сов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>plus sign</li>
<li>plus</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> advantage
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плюс.html>плю́сы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:минус.html>ми́нусы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pljúsy i mínusy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">pros and cons</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:плюхаться.html>плю́хаться</a> (27236)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">плюх</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pljux</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-a</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-tʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плюхаться.html>плю́хаться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pljúxatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плюхнуться.html>плю́хнуться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to flop <i>(down)</i>, to flop <i>(into)</i>, to plump <i>(into)</i>, to plop <i>(into)</i>, to drop <i>(into)</i>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">плюш</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pljuš</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-евый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-evyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плюшевый.html>плю́шевый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pljúševyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>plush
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:плюшевый.html>плю́шевый</a></b> ми́шка</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pljúševyj</b> míška</i> ― <span class="e-translation">teddy bear</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***плясать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:плясать.html>пляса́ть</a> (4580)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">плꙗсати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pljasati</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to dance</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*plęsati</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to dance</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐍀𐌻𐌹𐌽𐍃𐌾𐌰𐌽</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">plinsjan</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is a borrowing from some Slavic language.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плясать.html>пляса́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pljasátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сплясать.html>спляса́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to dance, to esp. to do folk dancing</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to caper, to hop</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to dance</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:танцевать.html>танцева́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">tancevátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***пневматический.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пневматический.html>пневмати́ческий</a> (25034)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">pneumatique</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-еский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-eskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пневматический.html>пневмати́ческий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pnevmatíčeskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> air; pneumatic <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">relating to air or other gases</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пневматический.html>пневмати́ческий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пистолет.html>пистоле́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pnevmatíčeskij</b> pistolét</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>air</b> pistol</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пневматический.html>пневмати́ческий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:молоток.html>молото́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pnevmatíčeskij</b> molotók</i> ― <span class="e-translation">nail gun</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>pneumatic</b> hammer</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пнуть.html>пнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пинать.html>пина́ть</a></b>)

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пнуть.html>пнуть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 3b✕.  <a href = vnd.unilang:образование.html>Образова́ние</a> страдального <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стия</a> прош. вр. <a href = vnd.unilang:затруднительный.html>затрудни́тельно</a>.    <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:пинать.html>пина́ть</a>.

***по.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> (16)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*po</i>, from Proto-Indo-European <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂pó</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition_4">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">po</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">with accusative case</span>
<ol><li>up to</li>
<li>till</li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">indicates distribution (with numerals other than one, a thousand, a million, a billion, a trillion, etc. and compound numerals ending these words)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>две</a>) / <b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:двести.html>две́сти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pó</b> dva (dve) / <b>po</b> dvésti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">two / two hundred each</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">with dative case</span>
<ol><li>along</li>
<li>over</li>
<li>around</li>
<li>about</li>
<li>on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плыть.html>плыть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:река.html>реке́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">plytʹ <b>po</b> reké</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to swim on a river</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>according to</li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">showing the cause that is unwanting or unwilling</span> (see из-за usage notes for more detail)</li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">indicates the direct object of some verbs of striking or hitting</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нанести.html>нанести́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:удар.html>уда́р</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ядерный.html>я́дерным</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:объект.html>объе́ктам</a> ира́на</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nanestí udár <b>po</b> jádernym obʺjéktam Irána</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to launch a strike at Iran's nuclear ambitions</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">indicates repetition of time</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:четверг.html>четверга́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>po</b> četvergám</i> ― <span class="e-translation">on Thursdays (every Thursday)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">indicates distribution (with numerals one, a thousand, a million, a billion, a trillion, etc. and compound numerals ending in these words)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одному́</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одно́й</a>) / <b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тысяча.html>ты́сяче</a> / <b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:миллион.html>миллио́ну</a> / <b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:миллиард.html>миллиа́рду</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>po</b> odnomú (odnój) / <b>po</b> týsjače / <b>po</b> milliónu / <b>po</b> milliárdu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">one / a thousand / a million / a billion each</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">with prepositional case</span>
<ol><li>on, immediately after
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:приезд.html>прие́зде</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>po</b> prijézde</i> ― <span class="e-translation">on arrival</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>for
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носить.html>носи́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:траур.html>тра́ур</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нём</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nositʹ traur <b>po</b> njóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">be in mourning for him</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to the liking of
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нём</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>po</b> njóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to his liking</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>When used with numerals in a distributive sense, the following should be noted:
<ul><li>The case of the numeral is the dative for the numerals one, a thousand, a million, a billion, a trillion, etc. and compound numerals ending in these words, e.g. twenty-one, but the accusative inanimate (even with animate nouns) for the remainder.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>да́л</a> им <b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пя́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рубль.html>рубле́й</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja dal im <b>po pjátʹ</b> rubléj.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I gave them <b>five</b> rubles <b>each</b>.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>да́л</a> им <b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:двадцать.html>двадцати́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одному́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рубль.html>рублю́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja dal im <b>po dvadcatí odnomú</b> rubljú.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I gave them <b>twenty-one</b> rubles <b>each</b>.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отправить.html>отпра́вили</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́ка</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">My otprávili <b>po trí</b> čelovéka.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">We sent <b>three</b> men <b>each</b>.</span> (<span class="e-source">note, not animate <b>*<a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>трёх</a></b></span>)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li>The case of an associated noun, if any, follows the normal rules for the numeral (dative singular for one and compounds ending in one; genitive singular for two, three, four and compounds ending in these numerals; and genitive plural in all other cases).</li>
<li>With <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tri</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сто.html>сто</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sto</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (but not compounds ending in these numerals), the stress is optionally drawn onto <b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a></b>:
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>да́л</a> им <b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a></b>/<b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рубль.html>рубля́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja dal im <b>pó dva</b>/<b>po dvá</b> rubljá.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I gave them <b>two</b> rubles <b>each</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мера.html>ме́ре</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>того́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">po mére tovó kak</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:предлог.html>Предло́г</a>; неизменяемое <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-по-</b>.

Their counterparts, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бежать.html>бежа́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bežátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:побежать.html>побежа́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pobežátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, are concrete verbs.

***победа.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:победа.html>побе́да</a> (1145)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">побѣда</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poběda</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">victory, defeat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:победа.html>побе́да</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pobéda</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:победа.html>побе́ды</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:победа.html>побе́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:победа.html>побе́д</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>victory</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:победить.html>победи́ть</a> (2424)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Related to the noun <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беда.html>беда́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bedá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">побѣдити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poběditi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">побије́дити</i>/<i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">pobijéditi</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">победя́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pobedjá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:победить.html>победи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pobedítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:побеждать.html>побежда́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to win, to be victorious over, to conquer, to vanquish, to defeat</li>
<li>to overcome</li>
<li>to beat</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>In the first person singular the phrase "<a href = vnd.unilang:одержать.html>одержа́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:победа.html>побе́ду</a>" is used instead.</li></ul>
